30  //package sun.nio.cs.ext;
31  
32  import java.nio.charset.Charset;
33  import java.nio.charset.CharsetDecoder;
34  import java.nio.charset.CharsetEncoder;
35  import java.nio.charset.CharacterCodingException;
36  import sun.nio.cs.HistoricallyNamedCharset;
37  
38  public class EUC_KR_OLD
39      extends Charset
40      implements HistoricallyNamedCharset
41  {
42      public EUC_KR_OLD() {
43          super("EUC-KR-OLD", null);
44      }
45  
46      public String historicalName() {
47          return "EUC_KR";
48      }
49  
50      public boolean contains(Charset cs) {
51          return ((cs instanceof EUC_KR_OLD)
52                  || (cs.name().equals("US-ASCII")));
53      }
54  
55      public CharsetDecoder newDecoder() {
56          return new Decoder(this);
57      }
58  
59      public CharsetEncoder newEncoder() {
60          return new Encoder(this);
61      }
62  
63  
64      /**
65       * These accessors are temporarily supplied while sun.io
66       * converters co-exist with the sun.nio.cs.{ext} charset coders
67       * These facilitate sharing of conversion tables between the
68       * two co-existing implementations. When sun.io converters
69       * are made extinct these will be unncessary and should be removed
70       */
71  
72      public short[] getDecoderIndex1() {
73          return Decoder.index1;
74      }
75  
76      public String[] getDecoderIndex2() {
77          return Decoder.index2;
78  
79      }
80  
81      public short[] getEncoderIndex1() {
82          return Encoder.index1;
83  
84      }
85      public String[] getEncoderIndex2() {
86          return Encoder.index2;
87  
88      }
